The black,navy, & browns will smear and then the teal,green,gold etc..will \\"set\\" just fine..so it's not based on \\"lighter/darker\\" colors at all, it's very random. However, ALL the colors are very pigmented and go on well with only 1-3 strokes depending on the thickness of the line you want..so that's a plus. If set with eyeshadow they last for at least 9 hrs and didn't need a touch-up before I removed them. I haven't yet tried them longer than that so I can't say what the true wear time can be. All in all...these are great for a fun & playful pop of color and the price point is really low so that it's no big loss if you don't like them or won't use them very much. They're worth the price just to have the lighter colors to experiment with and you can always use them as a base for eyeshadows to extend the life of your more expensive eye primers/bases, if nothing else.
